31b2(mdo sde): dag rjes su dran no// rjes su dran nas kyang de'i mtshan mo zad pa dang / rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen po nas byung ste/ srog chags stong phrag du ma dang lhan cig tu bya rgod phung po'i rig la
31b3(mdo sde): ba dang / bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste/ phyin nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas phyogs gcig tu
31b4(mdo sde): 'dug go// phyogs gcig tu 'dug nas/ byang chub sems dpa' mdzes pa'i tog gis/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ rmi lam na rnga'i sgra las bstan
31b5(mdo sde): pa'i tshigs su bcad pa gang dag thos pa de dag gsol to// nub gcig g.yel ba med par yang // bdag gi rmi lam rmis pa ni// mdzes pa'i rdo chen mthong ba ste// thams cad du ni gser gyi
31b6(mdo sde): 'od// nyi ma ji ltar bzhin du 'bar// kun tu rnam par lhung nge ste// phyogs bcu rnams su snang bar gyur// kun tu rin chen shing drung na// rin chen bai DUR+Ya dag gis// khri la sangs rgyas
31b7(mdo sde): rnams bzhugs te// brgya stong phrag ni du ma yi// 'khor dbus mdun gyis bltas pa mthong // bram ze'i gzugs kyi 'dra ba zhig/ rnga chen rab tu brdung ba mthong // de yis de la brdungs pa dang //
32a1(mdo sde): tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag byung // gser 'od dam pa'i rnga chen sgra yis ni// stong gsum 'jig rten 'jig rten gsum 'di na// dran song sdug bsngal gshin rje'i
32a2(mdo sde): sdug bsngal las// dbul ba'i sdug bsngal sdug bsngal zhi bar shog/ rnga bo che yi sgra skad 'di yis ni// 'jig rten rmongs pa thams cad zhi gyur cig/ ji ltar thub dbang 'jigs med 'dzin
32a3(mdo sde): zhi ltar// sems can 'jigs med 'jigs dang bral bar shog/ ji ltar 'khor bar kun mkhyen thub dbang po// 'phags pa'i yon tan kun dang ldan pa ltar// skye dgu ting 'dzin byang chub ya na
32a4(mdo sde): lag gi/ yon tan ldan zhing yon tan rgya mtshor gyur// rnga bo che yi sgra skad 'di yis ni// sems can thams cad tshangs pa'i sgra ldan gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub dam pa mchog reg shog
32a5(mdo sde): chos kyi 'khor lo dge ba skor gyur cig/ bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab bzhugs par shog/ 'gro la phan phyir chos kyang ston gyur cog/ nyon mongs 'joms gyur sdug bsngal sel bar
32a6(mdo sde): shog 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug zhi gyur cig/ sems can gang dag ngan song sar gnas te// rus pa'i lus la me lce rab 'bar ba// de dag rnga chen bsgrags pa thos gyur cig
32a7(mdo sde): sdug bsngal thams cad rab tu zhi gyur nas// sangs rgyas phyag 'tshal lo zhes tshig thos shog/ sems can kun gyi tshe rabs brgya dag dang // tshe rabs stong phrag bye ba skye dran shog/
32b1(mdo sde): thub pa'i dbang po rtag tu dran gyur cig/ de dag gis ni rgya chen gsung thos shog/ rnga bo che yi sgra skad 'di yis ni// sangs rgyas rnams dang rtag tu 'grogs rnyed gyur// sdig pa'i las
32b2(mdo sde): rnams rnam par spong bar shog/ bya ba dge ba rnams ni spyod gyur cig/ mi dang lha dang srog chags thams cad kyi// de dag bsam dang smon lam gang yin pa// rnga bo che mo sgra skad 'di yis ni/
32b3(mdo sde): de dag rnams kyi re kun rdzogs gyur cig/ sems can gang dag sems dmyal mi bzad skyes// lus la me lce kun tu rab tu 'bar// skyabs med mya ngan bcas shing yongs 'khyam pa// me rnams de dag
32b4(mdo sde): rab tu zhi bar shog/ sems dmyal yi dgas mi yi 'jig rten na// sems can sdug bsngal mi bzad drag po gang // rnga bo che yi sgra skad 'di yis ni// de dag rnams kyi sdug bsngal kun zhi
32b5(mdo sde): shog rten med dpung gnyen med pa dang // skyabs med par ni gyur pa dag/ de rnams la ni skyob pa dang // dpung gnyen rten mchog bdag gyur cig/ sangs rgyas rkang gnyis dam pa dag
32b6(mdo sde): thugs brtse thugs rje ldan pa'i thugs// gang dag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten na// bzhugs pa bdag la dgongs su gsol// bdag gis sngon chad sdig pa'i las// shin tu mi bzad gang
32b7(mdo sde): bgyis pa// stobs bcu'i spyan sngar bdag mchis te// de dag thams cad bshags par bgyi// pha ma dag tu mi 'dzin dang // sangs rgyas rnams su mi 'dzin dang // dge ba dag tu mi 'dzin dang /
33a1(mdo sde): sdig pa bdag gis gang bgyis dang // phyug pa'i rgyags pas dregs pa dang // rigs dang longs spyod rgyags pa dang // gzhon pa'i rgyags pas dregs pa yis/
33a2(mdo sde): bdag gis sdig pa gang bgyis dang // nyes bsams nyes par smras pa dang // nyes par bgyis pa'i las rnams dang // nyes pa'i dmigs su ma bltas pas// bdag gis sdig pa gang
33a3(mdo sde): bgyis dang // byis pa'i blo yi 'jug pa dang // mi shes mun pa'i sems dang ni// sdig pa'i grogs po'i dbang 'gyur dang // nyon mongs rnam par 'khrug sems dang // rtsed mo dga' ba'i dbang
33a4(mdo sde): nyid dang // mya ngan dang ni nad dbang dang // nor gyis mi mchog nyes pa yis// bdag gis sdig pa gang bgyis dang // 'phags min skye bo 'dre ba dang // phrag dog ser sna'i rgyu dang ni// g.yo dang dbul ba'i
33a5(mdo sde): nyes pa yis// bdag gis sdig pa gang bgyis dang // 'phongs pa byung ba'i dus kyi tshe// 'dod pa rnams kyi 'jigs rgyu dang // phyug po ma yin gyur pa yis// bdag gis sdig pa gang
33a6(mdo sde): bgyis dang // g.yo ba'i sems kyi dbang nyid dang // 'dod dang khro ba'i dbang dag dang // bkres dang skom gyis nyen pa yis// bdag gis sdig pa gang bgyis dang // bza' ba
33a7(mdo sde): ngag dang btung ba dang // bud med rgyu dang gos kyi phyir// nyon mongs gdung ba sna tshogs kyis// bdag gis sdig pa gang bgyis dang // lus dang ngag dang yid kyi sdig/ nyes par spyod pa rnam/
33b1(mdo sde): gsum bsags// 'di 'dra'i tshul gyis gang bgyis pa// de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// sangs rgyas rnams dang chos rnams dang // de bzhin nyan thos rnams la yang //
33b2(mdo sde): gus pa ma lags gang bgyis pa// de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// gang yang rang sangs rgyas rnams dang // byang chub sems dpa' rnams la yang // gus pa ma lags bgyis pa rnams//
33b3(mdo sde): de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// dam chos smra ba rnams la yang // gus pa ma lags bgyis pa dang // chos la'ang gus pa ma bgyis pa// de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// bdag gis rtag
33b4(mdo sde): tu mi shes pas// dam pa'i chos ni spangs pa dang // pha ma rnams la mgus dang // de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// blun pa dang ni byis pa dang // 'dod 'chags zhe sdang gti mug dang / nga rgyal
33b5(mdo sde): dregs pas bsgribs bgyis pa// de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// bdag ni phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten du// stobs bcu rnams la mchod par shog/ bdag ni phyogs bcur sems can
33b6(mdo sde): rnams// sdug bsngal kun las 'don gyur cig/ sems can bsam gyis mi khyab kun// sa bcu dag la 'god par shogs bcu dag la gnas nas kyang // thams cad de bzhin gshegs
33b7(mdo sde): gyur cig/ ji srid sdug bsngal rgya mtsho las// de kun thar bgyid nus srid du// sems can re re'i phyir yang ni// bskal pa bye bar spyod par shog/ gser 'od dam pa zhes bgyi ba/
34a1(mdo sde): las rnams thams cad byang byed pa// zab mo dag ni ston pa 'di// sems can de dag ston gyur cig/ gang gis bskal pa stong rnams su// sdig pa shin tu mi
34a2(mdo sde): bzad bgyis// lan cig rab tu bshags pa yis// de dag thams cad byang bar 'gyur// gang gis las kyi sgrib pa rnams// myur du yang dag zad 'gyur ba/ gser 'od dam pa dge ba yis//
34a3(mdo sde): bshags pa 'di dag bshags nas ni// rin chen 'byung gnas mchog bcu po// sa bcu la ni gnas par shog/ sangs rgyas yon tan snang gyur cig/ srid pa'i mtsho las sgrol bar shog/ sangs
34a4(mdo sde): rgyas rgya mtsho chu bo dang // yon tan rgya mtsho zab mo de// sangs rgyas yon tan bsam yas kyis// thams cad mkhyen du rdzogs par shog/ ting 'dzin brgya phrag stong rnams dang // gzungs rnams bsam
34a5(mdo sde): gyis mi khyab dang // dbang stobs byang chub yan lag gis// stobs bcu dam par 'gyur bar shog/ dgongs pa'i thugs kyis sangs rgyas rnams// bdag la rnam par gzigs su gsol// thugs
34a6(mdo sde): rjer ldan pa'i thugs kyis ni// nongs pa rab tu gzung du gsol// bdag gis bskal pa brgya rnams su// sngon chad sdig pa gang bgyis pa// de phyir bdag ni mya ngan sems// 'phongs dang mya
34a7(mdo sde): ngan 'jigs pas gzir// sdig pa'i las la 'jigs par bgyid// yid ni rtag tu dman par gyur// gang dang gang du 'gro bgyid pa// bdag ni gang du'ang dga' ma mchis// sangs rgyas
34b1(mdo sde): thams cad thugs rjer ldan// 'gro ba kun gyis 'jigs sel bas// nongs pa rab tu gzung du gsol// 'jigs pa dag las bdag thar mdzod// bdag gi nyon mongs las rnams kyi//
34b2(mdo sde): dri ma de bzhin gshegs pas shol// sangs rgyas rnams kyis bdag la ni// thugs rje'i chu yis bkru bar gsol// sdig pa thams cad bshags par bgyi// sngon chad bdag gis gang bgyis dang //
34b3(mdo sde): da ltar bdag gis sdig pa gang // de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// nongs par bgyis pa'i las rnams kun// slan chad mi bgyi bsdam par bgyi// bdag gis nongs par bgyis pa
34b4(mdo sde): gang / sdig de bcab par mi bgyi'o// lus kyi rnam par bsams pa dang // las rnams bcu po bgyis pa dag/ de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// lus kyis bgyis dang ngag gi las//
34b5(mdo sde): yid kyis rnam par bsams pa dang // las rnams bcu po bgyis pa dag/ de dag thams cad bdag 'chags so// mi dge ba bcu spangs nas ni// dge ba bcu po rten bgyis la/ sa bcu la
34b6(mdo sde): ni bdag gnas shing // stobs bcu mchog tu 'gyur bar shog/ bdag gi sdig pa'i las gang dag/ mi 'dod 'bras bu thob bgyid pa// sangs rgyas spyan sngar mchis nas su// de dag thams
34b7(mdo sde): cad bshags par bgyi// 'dzam du'i gling 'dir gang dag dang // 'jig rten khams ni gzhan dag tu// gang rnams dge ba'i las bgyid pa// de dag kun la yi rang ngo // lus dang ngag dang yid
35a1(mdo sde): kyis kyang // bdag gis bsod nams gang bsgrubs pa// bdag ni dge ba'i rtsa ba des// byang chub mchog la reg par shog/ srid 'gror 'am ngar byis pa'i blo yas ni/
35a2(mdo sde): shin tu mi bzang sdig pa gang bgyis pa// stobs bcu mi nyams spyan sngar mchis nas ni// sdig pa de kun so sor bshags par bgyi// skye ba nya mang srid pa namang dang // 'dzin rten nyam g.yo
35a3(mdo sde): sems nyam nga bar// lus kyi spyod pa nyam nga sna tshogs kyis// bdag gis sdig pa gang bsags de 'chags so// byis pa blun byas nyon mongs nyam nga dang // sdig pa'i grogs dang phrad pa nyam nga dang // /
35a4(mdo sde): srid pa nyam nga 'dod chags nyam nga dang // zhe sdang gti mug mun pa nyam nga dang // ngal ba'i nyam nga dus kyi nyam nga dang // bsod rnams bsgrubs pa nyam nga dag gis kyang // rgyal ba mi mnyam mngon sum
35a5(mdo sde): mchis nas su// sdig pa de kun so sor bshags par bgyi// sangs rgyas gser mdog ri snang ri rab 'dra// yon tan rgya mtsho 'dra la phyag 'tshal lo// rgyal ba de dag rnams la skyabs su mchi/
35a6(mdo sde): rgyal ba de dag rnams la mgos phyag 'tshal// gser mdog gser ni dri ma med pa'i gser gyi 'od// dri med rnam dag bai DUR+Ya yi yan lag spyan// sangs rgyas nyi ma dpal gzi grags 'bar 'byung
35a7(mdo sde): ba'i gnas// thugs rje'i 'od zer dag gis mun pa mun nag bsal// yan lag rab tu dri med rab bzang rnam par mdzes// sangs rgyas nyi ma yan lag dri med gser 'dras khyab/
35b1(mdo sde): nyon mongs mes gdungs yid can 'bar ba'i me 'dral// thub pa zla ba'i 'od zer dra bas tshim par mdzad/ mtshan mchog sum cu gnyis kyis dbang po yan lag mdzes// dpe byad bzang po dag gis/
35b2(mdo sde): yan lag rnam par mdzes// dpal gzi bsod nams 'bar 'khrugs 'od zer dra ba yis// 'jig rten gsum na mun khrod nyi mu bzhin du bzhugs// dri med rgya chen la dog sna tshogs bai DUR+Ya/
35b3(mdo sde): rengs dmar dung dngul dang shel bzhin yan lag dmar// 'od zer dra ba rnam pa sna tshogs legs brgyan pas// thub chen khyod ni nyi ma bzhin du de yis mdzes// mya ngan 'khrug pa pachi chu che ba'i rnga rlangs
35b4(mdo sde): can// 'khor ba'i klung chen 'phongs pa'i chu bor lhung ba la// sdug bsngal rgya mtsho mchog tu rtsub cing shugs drag pa// bde gshegs nyi ma'i 'od zer mang po rnams kyis bskams// yan lag gser
35b5(mdo sde): gyi mdog tu rnam par snang // ye shes 'byung gnas 'jig rten gsum kun mchog/ rab mdzes mtshan gyis yan lag rnam spras pa// sangs rgyas gser sku 'bar la phyag 'tshal lo// ji ltar rgya mtsho
35b6(mdo sde): chu ni dpag med dang // ji ltar sa las rdul mtha' yas dang // ji ltar rI rab rdo mtha' mtshungs med dang // ji ltar nam ma'i' mtha' yas pa// de bzhin sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas te/
35b7(mdo sde): sems can kun gyis shes par mi nus so// bskal pa du mar gzhal zhing bsam kyang ni// yon tan mtha' ma shes par mi nus so// nu ni skra yi rtse mo'i tshad tsham dang // rdor bcas rir bcas
36a1(mdo sde): mtshor bcas pa ni// bskal pa bgrangs na shes par nus kyang srid// sangs rgyas yon tan shes par mi nus so// yon tan kha dog snyan dang grags pa dang // dge
36a2(mdo sde): ba'i mtshan gyis brgyan pa'i sku lus dang // dpe byad bzang po brgyad cus brgyan pa yis// sems can thams cad de 'drar gyur par shog/ bdag ni dge ba'i las rnams 'di dag gis// 'jig rten
36a3(mdo sde): mi ring sangs rgyas 'gyur bar shog/ 'gro la phan phyir chos kyang ston gyur cig/ sems can sdug bsngal mang gzir thar byed shog/ stobs bcas sder bcas bdud las rgyal gyur cig/ chos kyi 'khor
36a4(mdo sde): lo dge bskor bar shog/ bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab gnas gyur cig/ bdud rtsi'i chu yis sems can tshim byed shog/ ji ltar sngon gyi rgyal ba'i rdzogs pa ltar// pha rol phyin drug bla med rdzogs
36a5(mdo sde): par shog/ nyon mongs bcom zhing sdug bsngal sel gyur cig/ 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug zhi byed shog/ tshe rabs brgya dang tshe rabs bye ba stong // bdag ni rtag tu tshe rabs dran par shog/ thub
36a6(mdo sde): pa'i dbang po rtag tu dran gyur cig/ de dag rnams kyi gsung rgya che thos shog/ bdag ni dge ba'i las rnams 'di dag gis/ rtag tu sangs rgyas 'grogs pa rnyed par shog
36a7(mdo sde): sdig pa'i las rnams rnam par spong gyur cig/ dge ba'i 'byung gnas dge rnams spyod par shog/ zhing rnams kun nas srog chags thams cad kyang // 'jig rten dag na sdug
36b1(mdo sde): bsngal kun nor gyur// sems can dbang po mtshang yan lag nyams// de kun di ring dbang po tshang bar shog/ gang dag nang btab kun chung lus rnams dang // phyogs bcu dag na
36b2(mdo sde): skyabs med gyur pa rnams// de kun myur du nad las thar gyur cig/ nad med stobs dang dbang po rnyed par shog/ gang dug rgyal po chom kun dgras bsdigs gsang thug dang // sdug bsngal rnam pa sna
36b3(mdo sde): tshogs brgya yis 'phongs gyur pa// sems can nyam thag gyur cing sdug bsngal de dag kun// 'jigs tshogs mi bzad brgyad po de las thar gyur cig/ gang dag brdegs shing bcing
36b4(mdo sde): bas bcings gzir ba// 'phongs pa sna tshogs dag na gnas gyur cing // nyon mongs stong phrag du mas dkrugs nas kyang // 'jigs pa mi bzad mya ngan sna tshogs rnyed// de dag thams cad
36b5(mdo sde): bcings las grol gyur cig/ rdeg pa dag ni brdeg las thar bar shog/ gsad pa rnams kyang srog dang ldan gyur cig/ 'phongs gyur thams cad 'jigs pa med par shog/ sems can
36b6(mdo sde): gang dag bkres sred skom gyis gzir// de dag zas skom sna tshogs rnyed par shog/ long bas gzugs rnams sna tshogs mthong gyur cig/ 'on pas yid 'ong sgra rnams thos par shog
36b7(mdo sde): gcer bu rnams kyis sna tshogs gos rnyed gyur// sems can dngul pos gter rnams snyed par shog/ nor 'bru rin chen sna tshogs mang po yos// sems can thams cad bde dang ldan par shog
37a1(mdo sde): gang yang sdug bsngal tshor bas gnod ma gyur// sems can thams cad blta na sdug pa dang // gzugs bzang mdzes shing tshul du shis par shog/ rtag tu bde ba du
37a2(mdo sde): ma sogs gyur cig/ yid kyis zas skom rab 'byor bsod nams dag/ bsams ma thag tu de dag grub gyur cig/ rdza rnga cang te'u pi wang sgra snyan dang // chu mig mtsho dang rdzing bu lteng ka dag
37a3(mdo sde): gser gyi pad+ma ut+pal 'dab ma can// zas skom gos nor mu tig nor bu dbyig/ rgyan gser rin chen sna tshogs bai DUR+Ya// de dag bsams ma thag tu grub gyur cig/ 'jig rten gang nu'ang sdug bsngal
37a4(mdo sde): sgra ma byung // sems can gcig kyang mi 'phrod mthong ma gyur// de dag thams cad kha dog rgya chen dang // phan tshun du ni 'od byed gyur par shog/ mi yi 'jig rten phun sum tshogs gang yod//
37a5(mdo sde): de dag bsams par skye bar de dag gyur// bsams pa thams cad bsams ma thag tu yang // bsod nams 'bras bu yongs su rdzogs par shog/ spos dang 'phreng ba dag dang byug
37a6(mdo sde): pa dang // gos dang phye ma me tog sna tshogs dang // ljon shing gang las dus gsum 'bab par shog/ sems can de dag len cing dgar gyur cig/ de bzhin gshegs pa bsam
37a7(mdo sde): las thams cad dang // rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos dang // rdul bral dri med brtan pa'i chos la yang // phyogs bcu rnams su mchod pa byed par shog/ 'gro ba dman pa
37b1(mdo sde): thams cad sbyong gyur cig/ mi khom brgyad po dag las 'das par shog/ dal ba'i rgyal po dam pa mchog thob gyur// rtag tu sangs rgyas 'grogs pa thob par shog/ rtag tu mthon po'i
37b2(mdo sde): rigs su skye bar shog/ nor dang 'bru yi mdzod rnams 'byor gyur cig/ sman+da dang grags dang gzugs dang kha dog gis// bskal pa du mar legs par brgyan par shog/ bud med thams cad
37b3(mdo sde): rtag tu phor gyur te// dpa' zhing rtul po mkhas shing gsal bar shog/ de kun rtag tu byang chub phyir spyod gyur// pha rol phyin pa drug la spyod par shog/ phyogs bcu dag na rin chen shing
37b4(mdo sde): dbang drung // sangs rgyas bde bzhugs rin chen bai DUR+Ya'i// khri la bzhugs pa dag ni mthong gyur cig/ chos bsnun pa yang de dag thos par shog/ bdag gis sdig pa'i las rnams
37b5(mdo sde): bsgrubs pa ni// srid pa nyam ngar sngon chad gang bsgrubs pa// sdig las gang dag mi 'dod 'bras thob pa// de dag thams cad ma lus zad gyur cig/ sems can gang dag srid par bcing
37b6(mdo sde): nas kun// 'khor ba'i zhags pa'i thag pas dam bcings pa// shes rab lag gis bcings pa khrol bar shog/ sdug bsngal rnams las thar gyur thob gyur cig/ sems can gang dag
37b7(mdo sde): 'dzam bu'i gling 'di dang / gang dag 'jig rten khams ni gnan rnams na// bsod nams sna tshogs zab mo rnams byed pa// de dag kun la rjes su yi rang ngo // lus dang ngag dang yid kyis bsnyungs pa
38a1(mdo sde): yis/ bdag gis rjes su yi rangs bsod nams des// bdag gis smon grub 'bras bu yod par shog/ byang chub rdul bral bu med thob gyur cig/ gang dag rtug dang dri ma/
38a2(mdo sde): bral ba dang // dri med yid kyis phyag 'tshal bstod pa dang // yongs su bsngo ba brjod pa 'di yis ni// bskal pa drug cur ngan song spong bar gyur// tshigs su bcad pa brjod pa 'di dag gis//
38a3(mdo sde): skyes pa bud med bram ze rgyal rigs las// thal sbyar 'dug ste rgyal ba gang bstod pa// tshe rabs kun tu skye ba dran par 'gyur// yan lag dbang po kun gyi yan lag brgyan// bsod nams
38a4(mdo sde): yon tan sna tshogs rnams dang ldan// mi dbang rgyal pos rtag tu de mchod de// de dang de dag tu ni de 'drar 'gyur// gang dag rna ba'i bu grwar bshags pa 'di na grags gyur pa// de dag
38a5(mdo sde): sangs rgyas gcig gi gan nas dge ba byas ma yin// gnyis la ma yin bzhi la ma yin lnga min bcu la min// de ltar sangs rgyas stong gi gan nas dge ba byas ma yin// de'i tshe bcom
38a6(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyis tshigs su bcad po de dag gsan nas// byang chub sems dpa' mdzes pa'i tog la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// legaso legs so// rigs kyi bu khyod kyi rmi laman//
38a7(mdo sde): gser gyi rnga las de bzhin gshegs pa'i yang dag pa'i yon tan bsngags pa dang / sdig pa bshags pa 'di dag gang gis thos pa de dag thams cad bsod nams kyi phung po rgya chen po dang ldan pa dang /
38b1(mdo sde): skye bo mang po la phan pa dang / bde bas tshim par byed de/ sgrib pa thams cad byang bar 'gyur bar shes par gyis shig/ 'di lta bu'i spyod pa khyad par can dang ldan pa 'di dag ni thams cad kyang sngon/
38b2(mdo sde): 'das pa'i dus na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dag la bstod pa dang / smon lam rgya chen po btab pa'i rgyu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis de dag thos par gyur pa yin no zhes bka' stsal
38b3(mdo sde): nas/ de nas 'khor 'dus pa de dag thams cad bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// / gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po lasarmi lam na
38b4(mdo sde): bshags pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das yang dag par rnam par dbye ba la bzhugs te/ shin tu zab mo mchog tu gyur pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
38b5(mdo sde): par zhugs ma thag tu/ sku'i ba spu'i bu gnas 'od zer kha dog rnam pa sna tshogs brgya stong tshad med pa byung bas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad 'od de'i nang du snang bar gyur pa ni/ phyogs bcu'i gang+gA
38b6(mdo sde): klung gi bye ma snyed kyis kyang dpe dang tshad kyis bskrun par mi nus so// sdigs ma lnga'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'od zer des snang bar gyur pa'i sems can de dag mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam dang / mtshams
38b7(mdo sde): med pa lnga byed pa dang / dkon mchog gsum la skur pa 'debs pa dang / bla ma dang gnyin pa la sri zhu chung ba dang / slob dpon dang / bram ze la bkur sti mi byed pa rnams/ sems can dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro dang /
39a1(mdo sde): yi dgas kyi gnas su lhung bar gyur pa de dag gi gnas su 'od des reg ma thag tu bde ba so sor myong bar gyur to// gang gis 'od de mthong ba dang / 'od de'i mthus thams
39a2(mdo sde): cad kyang bde zhing nyams dga' ba dang / kha dog dang dbyibs legs pa'i mchog thob pas mtshan phun sum tshogs pa dang / bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi tshogs rgyan dang ldan pas/ de bzhin
39a3(mdo sde): gshegs pa rnams mthong bar 'gyur ro// de nas brgya byin lha'i dbang po lha'i tshogs mang po dang / gang+gA'i lha mo la sogs te/ 'khor 'dus pa de dag ya mtshan du gyur pa'i 'od des bskul
39a4(mdo sde): nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der dong ste/ phyin nas bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa
39a5(mdo sde): ti'i bu stan las langs te/ bla gros phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bcom
39a6(mdo sde): ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo nyan thos kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la yang dag
39a7(mdo sde): par zhugs pa 'am/ theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ sems can gzhan dag kyang rung ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang
39b1(mdo sde): rgyu bar 'tshal bas/ las kyi sgrib pa rnams ji ltar so sor bshags par dgyi/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bu la 'di gad ces bka' stsam/
39b2(mdo sde): tau/ shA ri'i bu 'di la rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo nyan thos kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ theg pa chen po la
39b3(mdo sde): yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ sems can gzhan dag kyang rung ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs pa'i 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas nyin lan gsum mtshan lan gsum du/

39b6(mdo sde): phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten na/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu skor ba/ chos kyi 'khor
39b7(mdo sde): lo rab tu ston pa/ chos kyi tshul rab tu 'dzin pa/ chos kyi sbyin pa rab tu mdzad pa/ chos kyi sgron me rab tu 'bar bar mdzad pa/ chos kyi char rab tu 'bebs pa
40a1(mdo sde): chos kyi rnga rab tu rdung ba/ chos kyi rnga bo che rab tu rdung ba/ chos kyi dung rab tu 'bud pa dang / chos kyi srog shing sgreng ba sems can thams cad la chos kyi
40a2(mdo sde): sbyin pas tshim par mdzad pa/ nyam bag tu spyod du 'dzud pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la phyag 'tshal lo// / bam po gsum pa/
40a3(mdo sde): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mchod pa'i gnas/ phyag bgyi ba'i gnas/ mkhyen par gyur pa/ spyan du gyur pa/ dbang du gyur pa/ tshad mar gyur pa/ mkhyen pa dang ldan pa/

43a1(mdo sde): thos dbang che bar grags pa 'am/ rang byang chub mngon sum du byed par 'dod pa des kyang / 'di bzhin du las kyi sgrib pa rnams so sor bshags par bya'o// mi

43a4(mdo sde): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ shA ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pas chos thams cad ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'o// zhes gsungs pa'i phyir te/ rgyu dang rkyen gzhan dang / gzhon gyis gzhan skye'o// gzhan 'gag
43a5(mdo sde): go/ de la 'das pa'i chos gang yin pa de dag ni 'gag pa/ zad pa dang bral ba rnam pa ste/ de dag la yang las kyi sgrib pa cung zad kyang med do// de lhur na 'du byed pa gang yin po rnams kyang med pa
43a6(mdo sde): las byung ba ste/ de dag la yang las kyi sgrib pa cung zad kyang med do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ shA ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pas chos thams cad ni stong pa/ sems can med pa/ srog med pa/
43a7(mdo sde): gang zag med pa/ ma skyes pa/ ma 'gags pa/ 'dus ma byas pa zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro// shA ri'i bu chos thams cad bdag las byung yang bdag kyang yod pa ma yin no// shA ri'i bu rigs kyi
43b1(mdo sde): bu mo gang la la zhig 'di lta ste/ sems can med pa'i mtha'i chos kyi tshul 'di la 'jug pa 'di ni/ las kyi sgrib pad+hAnA gcod pa zhes bya ste/ shA ri'i bu 'di ni so sor bshags pa'o// de nas
43b2(mdo sde): yang bcom ldan 'das la/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu 'am/ rogs kyi bu mnyan thos kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa'am//
43b3(mdo sde): rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ sems can gzhan dag kyang rung ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
43b4(mdo sde): tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'tshal bas ji ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la rjes su yi rang bar bgyi/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa
43b5(mdo sde): shA ri'i bu la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ri'i bu 'dri la rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mos nyin lan gsum mtshan lan gsum du bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar la pus
43b6(mdo sde): mo g.yas pa'i lhang sa la btsugs te/ thal mo sbyar nas tshig 'di skad du phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten na/ sems can gang su dag sbyin pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bgyi ba'i dngos po dang /
43b7(mdo sde): tshul khrims las byung ba dang bsgom pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bgyi ba'i dngos po mngon par 'du bgyis pa/ de dag thams cad la yang rjes su yi rang ba'i mchog gis rjes su yi
44a1(mdo sde): rang ngo // rjes su yi rang ba dam pa dang / gtso bo dang / khyad par can dang / rab dang / phul dang / gya nom pa dang / bla ma dang / bla na med pa dang
44a2(mdo sde): lhag na med pa dang / mnyam pa med pa dang / mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pas rjes su yi rang ngo // phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten na/ sems can gang su dag sbyin pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bgyi
44a3(mdo sde): ba'i dngos po dang / tshul khrims las byung ba dang / bsgom pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bgyi ba'i dngos po mngon par 'du bgyid par 'gyur ba/ de dag thams cad la yang rjes su yi rang
44a4(mdo sde): ba'i mchog gis rjes su yi rang ba nas/ rjes su yi rang ba mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i bar gyis rjes su yi rang ngo // phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten na/ sems can gang su dag sbyin pa las byung /
44a5(mdo sde): ba'i bsod nams bgyi ba'i dngos po dang / tshul khrims las byung ba dang / bsgom pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bgyi ba'i dngos po mngon par bgyid pa de dag thams cad la yong rjes su ma
44a6(mdo sde): rang ba'i mchog gis rjes su yi rang ba nas/ rjes su yi rang ba mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i bar gyis rjes su yi rang ngo // byang chub sems dpa' gang dag da ltar na/ sems dang po bskyed pa de
44a7(mdo sde): dag gi dang po byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba gang lags pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' bskal pa brgyas 'byung ba rnams kyi bsod nams kyi phung po gang lags pa dang / byang
44b1(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob pa rnams kyi bsod nams kyi phung po gang lags pa dang / phyir mi ldog pa rnams kyi bsod nams kyi phung po gang lags pa dang / byang chub sems
44b2(mdo sde): dpa' skye ba gcig gis thogs pa rnams kyi bsod nams kyi phung po gang lags pa de dag thams cad la yang rjes su yi rang ba'i mchog gis rjes su yi rang ba nas/ rjes su yi rang ba mi mnyam pa dang
44b3(mdo sde): mnyam pa'i bar gyis rjes su yi rang ngo // byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa na/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba
44b4(mdo sde): mngon par 'dus bgyis pa gang lags pa de dag thams cad la rjes su yi rang ba'i mchog gis yi rang ngo // rjes su yi rab ba dam pa dang / gtso bo dang / khyad par can dang / rab dang / phul dang /
44b5(mdo sde): gya nom pa dang / bla ma dang / bla na med pa dang / lhag na med pa dang / mnyam pa med pa dang / mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pas rjes su yi rang ngo // ma 'ongs pa'i dus kyi byang chub sems dpa' sems
44b6(mdo sde): dpa' chen po de dag byang chub kyi phyir spyad pa spyod pa na/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug dang ldan pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po mngon par 'du bgyid par 'gyur ba gang lags pa de dag thams cad la yang rjes
44b7(mdo sde): su yi rang ba'i mchog gis rjes su yi rang ngo // rjes su yi rang ba dam pa dang / gtso bo dang / khyad par can dang / rab dang / phul dang sha gya nom dang / bla ma dang bla na med pa dang / ltag na med/
45a1(mdo sde): pa dang / mnyam pa med pa dang / mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pas rjes su yi rang ngo // byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang dag da ltar phyogs bcu'i 'jig
45a2(mdo sde): rten na/ byang chub kyi phyir spyod pa de dag pha rol tu phyin pa drug dang ldan pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po mngon par 'du bgyid pa gang lags pa de dag thams cad la yang rjes su yi rang ba'i mchog gis/
45a3(mdo sde): rjes su yi rang ngo // rjes su yi rang ba dam pa dang / gtso bo dang / khyad par can dang / rab dang / phul dang / gya nom pa dang / bla ma dang / bla na med pa dang / lhag na med pa dang / mnyam pa med pa dang /
45a4(mdo sde): mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pas rjes su yi rang ngo // skye bo mang po la sman pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba dang / skye bo phal po che dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang /
45a5(mdo sde): sman pa dang bde ba'i slad du/ sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag gis// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par
45a6(mdo sde): sangs rgyas nas/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bstan pa/ chos kyi tshul rab tu bzung ba/ chos kyi char rab tu phab pa/ chos kyi char rab tu btang ba/ chos kyi rnga rab
45a7(mdo sde): tu brdungs pa/ chos kyi rnga bo che brdungs pa/ chos kyi dung bus pa/ chos kyis srog shing bsgreng ba/ chos kyi sgron ma 'bar bar mdzad pa/ sems can thams cad la chos kyi sbyin pas tshim par
45b1(mdo sde): mdzad pa/ nyam bag tu spyod du 'dzud pa gang lags pa dang / de la nyan thos kyi theg pa pa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa 'am/ de las gzhan
45b2(mdo sde): pa'i sems can rnams kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa gang lags pa de dag thams cad la yang rjes su yi rang ba'i mchog gis rjes su yi rang ba nas rjes su yi rang ba mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i
45b3(mdo sde): bar gis rjes su yi rang ngo // skye bo mang po la sman pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba dang / skye bo phal po che dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang / sman pa dang
45b4(mdo sde): bde ba'i slad du/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus kyi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas chos kyi 'khor lo skor
45b5(mdo sde): bar 'gyur ba'i bar dag gang lags pa dang / de la nyan thos kyi theg pa pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa 'am de las gzhan
45b6(mdo sde): pa'i sems can gang dag dge ba'i rtsa ba skyed par 'gyur ba gang lags pa de dag thams cad la yang rjes su yi rang ba'i mchog gis rjes su yi bya nas rjes su yi rang ba mi mnyam pa dang mnyam
45b7(mdo sde): pa'i bar gyis rjes su yi rang ngo // skye bo mang po la sman pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba dang / skye bo bal po che dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi
46a1(mdo sde): don dang sman pa dang bde ba'i slad du/ da ltar phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten nu/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang /
46a2(mdo sde): chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu ston pa/ chos kyi tshul rab tu 'dzin pa/ chos kyi char rab tu 'bebs pa/ chos
46a3(mdo sde): kyi char rab tu gtong ba/ chos kyi sbyin pa sbyin par mdzad pa/ chos kyi sgron ma 'bar bar mdzad pa/ chos kyi rnga brdung ba dang / chos kyi rnga bo che brdung ba/ chos kyi dung 'bud pa/ chos kyi srog
46a4(mdo sde): shing bsgreng ba sems can thams cad la chos kyi sbyin pas tshim par mdzad pa/ nyam bag tu spyod du 'dzud pa gang lags pa dang / de la nyan thos kyi theg pa pa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas
46a5(mdo sde): kyi theg pa pa 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa 'am/ de las gzhan pa'i sems can de dag dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa gang lags pa de dag thams cad la yang rjes su yi rang ba'i mchog
46a6(mdo sde): gris rjes su yi rang ba nas rjes su yi rang ba mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i bar gyis rjes su yi rang ngo zhes brjod par bya'o// shA ri'i bu 'di ni rjes su yi rang ba'i bsod nams kyi phung po'o//
46a7(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo rjes su yi rang ba'i bsod nams kyi phung po 'dis rjes su yi rang na/ bsod nams kyi phung po mang po grangs med dpag tu med pa bskyed do// shA ri'i bu
46b1(mdo sde): stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sems can nas 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi sems can ji snyed pa de dag thams cad dgra bcom pa zag pa zad par gyur
46b2(mdo sde): la rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig gis de dag la ji srid 'tsho'i bar du gos dang / zas dang / na ba'i gsos sman dang / yo byad rnams kyis bsnyen bkur
46b3(mdo sde): byas pa bas gang zhig rjes su yi rang ba 'dis rjes su yi rang na/ de ni de bas bsod nams ches mang du grangs med dpag tu med pa bskyed do// shA ri'i bu de lta bas na/ rigs kyi bu 'am/
46b4(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu mo bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas/ rjes su yi rang ba 'dis rjes su yi rang bar bya'o// bud med skyes pa'i dbang
46b5(mdo sde): po thob par 'dod cing / bud med kyi dbang po brje bar 'dod pas kyang / rjes su yi rang ba 'dis rjes su yi rang bar bya'o// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la/ tshe dang /
46b6(mdo sde): ldan pa shA ri'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ma 'ongs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams la snang ba bgyis par 'gyur ba dang / da ltar byung ba'i
46b7(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis mos pa skyed par 'gyur ba'i bskul ba'i phung po yang bshad du gsol/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bu
47a1(mdo sde): la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ri'i bu 'di la rigs kyi bu mo nyan thos kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la yang dag par
47a2(mdo sde): zhugs pa 'am theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa'am/ sems can gzhan dag kyang rung ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod
47a3(mdo sde): pas nyin lan gsum mtshan lan gsum du bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar la/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ thal mo sbyar nas tshig 'di skad du/ sangs rgyas bcom
47a4(mdo sde): ldan 'das gang dag da ltar na phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams na/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa de dag la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs
47a5(mdo sde): rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la phyag 'tshal nas/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor bar bskul gyis/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis skye bo mang po la sman pa dang / skye bo mang
47a6(mdo sde): po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba dang / skye bo phal po che dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang / sman pa dang bde ba'i slad du/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor du gsol//
47a7(mdo sde): chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bstan du gsol/ chos kyi tshul rab tu gzung du gsol/ chos kyi sbyin pa mdzad du gsol/ chos kyi sgron ma 'bar bar mdzad du gsol/ chos kyi char dbab tu
47b1(mdo sde): gsol/ chos kyi char gtang du gsol/ chos kyi rnga brdung du gsol/ chos kyi rnga bo che brdung du gsol/ chos kyi dung 'bud du gsol/ chos kyi srog shing bsgreng du gsol ba zhes
47b2(mdo sde): brjod par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo nyan thos theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa
47b3(mdo sde): 'am theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ sems can gzhan dag kyang rung ste/ nyin lan gsum mtshan lan gsum du bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas
47b4(mdo sde): pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ thal mo sbyar nas tshig 'di skad du/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang dag da ltar na phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams na/ sku tshe'i 'du byed gtong ba'i
47b5(mdo sde): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la phyag 'tshal nas/ gsol ba 'debs kyis/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag skye
47b6(mdo sde): bo mang po la sman pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba dang / skye bo phal po che dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang / sman pa dang / bde ba'i slad du/ chos kyi 'khor lo
47b7(mdo sde): ni rab tu bskor// chos kyi sgron ma ni rab tu 'bar bar mdzad/ chos kyi char ni rab tu 'bebs/ chos kyi char ni rab tu gtong / chos kyi rnga ni rab tu brdung / chos kyi rnga bo che ni rab tu brdung
48a1(mdo sde): chos kyi dung ni rab tu 'bud/ chos kyi srog shing ni rab tu bsgreng / chos kyi sgron ma ni mchod par mdzad// sems can thams cad la chos kyi sbyin pas ni tshim
48a2(mdo sde): par mdzad/ nyam bag tu 'dzud cing / re zhig bzhugs su gsol/ gsol ba btab pa'i phung po 'di yang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngos te/ ji ltar
48a3(mdo sde): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo ba de bzhin du 'di yongs su bsngo'o zhes brjod par bya'o// shA ri'i bu 'di ni gsol ba gdab pa'i phung po ste/ rigs kyi bu 'am/
48a4(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu mo gsol ba gdab pa'i phung po 'dis gsol ba 'debs na/ bsod nams mang po grangs med dpag tu med pa bskyed do// shA ri'i bu rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig gis
48a5(mdo sde): stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams ji snyed pa de dag rin po che sna bdun gyis bkang ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la dbul ba phul ba bas// gang gis de bzhin gshegs pa de dag
48a6(mdo sde): la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bskul na/ de ni de bas bsod nams ches mang du grangs med dpag tu med pa bskyed do// shA ri'i bu stong gsum gyi spyod chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams lnga zhog ste/
48a7(mdo sde): shA ri'i bu 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dang mnyam pa ji snyed pa de dag rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig gis rin po che sna bdun gyis bkang ste/ de bzhin
48b1(mdo sde): gshegs pa rnams la dbul ba phul ba bas gang gis de bzhin gshegs pa de dag la gsol ba btab na/ de ni de bas bsod nams ches mang du grangs med dpag tu med pa bskyed
48b2(mdo sde): do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ shA ri'i bu ngas sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa na/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba btab ste/ dge ba'i
48b3(mdo sde): rtsa ba des na nga la lha'i dbang po brgya byin dang / mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pas bcom ldan 'das skye bo mang po la sman pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba dang /
48b4(mdo sde): skye bo phal po che dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang / sman pa dang / bde ba'i slad du/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor bar gsol zhes chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor bar gsol ba

48b6(mdo sde): gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dang / so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang / byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po dang / yongs su mya ngan las
48b7(mdo sde): 'das pa thob ste/ nga'i dam pa'i chos kyang yun ring du gnas par 'gyur ro// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bus yang 'di skad ces gsol to//
49a1(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo nyan thos kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa'am
49a2(mdo sde): theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa 'am/ sems can gzhan dag kyang rung ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'tshal bas thams
49a3(mdo sde): cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'gyur bar bgyi ba'i slad du/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams ji ltar yongs su bsngo bar bgyi/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bu la 'di//

49a6(mdo sde): nyin lan gsum mtshan lan gsum du tshig 'di skad ces thog ma dang tha ma ma mchis pa'i 'khor na 'khor ba'i tshe/ bdag gis dge ba'i rtsa ba mngon par 'dus bgyis par gyur pa/ sangs
49a7(mdo sde): rgyas sam/ chos sam/ dge 'dun nam/ gang zag gam/ tha na dud 'gro'i skye gnas su song ba rnams sam/ sems can gzhan dag kyang rung ste/ zan chang gcig tsam stsal bar gyur pa
49b1(mdo sde): dang 'chags pa gang lags pa dang / gsol ba gdab pa gang lags pa dang / skyabs su mchi ba gang lags pa dang / bslab pa'i gzhi dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba gang lags pa dang
49b2(mdo sde): so sor 'chags pa dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba gang lags pa dang / rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i bsod nams bgyi ba'i dngos po gang lags pa dang / gsol ba gdab pa dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i
49b3(mdo sde): rtsa ba gang lags pa de dag thams cad gcig tu bsdus/ gzhal bzlums te/ sems zhing rnam par grol ba dang / gzung ba ma mchis pas sems can thams cad la stsal to// ji ltar
49b4(mdo sde): dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams sems can thams cad la gtang bar bgyi ba/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes chags pa mi mnga' bas ji ltar mkhyen pa de lta
49b5(mdo sde): khus bdag gis dge ba'i rtsa ba de gtang ngo // sems can thams cad lag na rin po che dang ldan par gyur cig/ nam mkha'i mdzod dang / longs spyod zad mi shes pa dang / bsod
49b6(mdo sde): nams zad mi shes pa dang / chos zad mi shes pa dang / ye shes zad mi shes pa dang / spobs pa zad mi shes pa dang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs

56b2(mdo sde): sems bskyed pa bdun pa ni/ ded dpon mdzod chen pos phyug pa lta bur 'khor ba'i 'brog dgon pa las sgrol ba'i tshul gyis/ bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pas/
56b3(mdo sde): la legs par brgyan pa lta bur blta ste/ de la rgyu ni thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// sems bskyed pa brgyad pa ni/ zla ba nya'i dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa'i da bo'i tshul gyis//
56b4(mdo sde): sgrib pa thams cad rnam par dag pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa lta bur blta ste/ de la rgyu ni smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// sems bskyed pa dgu pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su
56b5(mdo sde): dag pa'i yon tan gyi rgyun bkod pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor gyi tshul gyis/ bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa byed pa lta bur blta ste/ de la rgyu ni stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// sems
56b6(mdo sde): bskyed pa bcu pa ni/ yon tan dang / ye shes dang / chos thams cad la dbang sgyur bar dbang bskur ba thob pas/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i mtshan gyi dpe'i tshul gyis/ nam mkha'i dang mtshungs
56b7(mdo sde): ba lta bur lnga ste/ de la rgyu ni ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa ni bcu po 'di dag yin te/ 'di dag dang ldan pas byang chub sems
57a1(mdo sde): dpa' zhes bya'o// don dam par na 'di la byang chub kyang med/ byang chub sems dpa' yang med/ byang chub kyi sems kyang med do// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub
57a2(mdo sde): sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dad pa'i dbang po sngon du 'gro ba dang / bsam pa sngon du 'gro/
57a3(mdo sde): ba dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / byams pa chen po sngon du 'gro ba dang / snying rje chen po sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can gyi rten
57a4(mdo sde): sngon du 'gro ba dang / bsdu ba'i dngos po sngon du 'gro ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos 'dod pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'dod pa sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byung
57a5(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu'o// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i na
57a6(mdo sde): du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ lus kyi las yongs su dag pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / ngag gi las yongs su dag pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / yid kyi las yongs su dag pa
57a7(mdo sde): rnon du 'gro dang / rnam par ma'i bsngon du 'gro ba dang / ngan song thams cad rnam par spong bsngon du 'gro ba dang / mi 'om pa brgyad rnam der slong bsngon du 'grong dang / nyan thos dang
57b1(mdo sde): rang sangs rgyas kyis las bzla ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan la bkod pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / bsam pa yongs su rdzogs pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sngon lam yongs su
57b2(mdo sde): rdzogs pa sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa 'di bcu'o// rigs kyi du la byang chub sems
57b3(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa ban+d+ha ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ rjes su chags pa spong ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / khyong khro ba sbyang ba sngon du/
57b4(mdo sde): 'gro ba dang / lus la mi lta ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / srog la yid mi ston pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / mos pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba sngon du 'gro ba dang
57b5(mdo sde): byams pa'i stobs sngon du 'gro ba dang / zab mos chos la bzod pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / rgya chen po la mos pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / mi shes pa bsal ba sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang
57b6(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnams pa bcu'o// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu
57b7(mdo sde): pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can thams cad kyi ci yod snyam pa sngon du 'gro ba dang dge ba'i lus dang
58a1(mdo sde): ngag dang / yid mngon par bsgrub pa la rjes su yi rang ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / zhum pa med pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i sa bsdu ba thob par bya ba
58a2(mdo sde): sngon du 'gro ba dang / yang dag pa'i rtsol ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / nyon mongs pa'i dgra 'dul ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams cad kyis dbyen/
58a3(mdo sde): pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yang dag par bsgrub pa sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub
58a4(mdo sde): sems dpa' rnams kyi brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu'o// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu
58a5(mdo sde): phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dge ba'i chos la gnas pa ston du 'gro ba dang / ting nge 'dzin sngon du 'gro ba dang / snyoms par 'jug paste/
58a6(mdo sde): du 'grong dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub sngon du 'gro ba dang ka bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang po sngon du 'gro ba dang / ting nge 'dzin/
58a7(mdo sde): gyi stongs sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi nyoni mongs pa spong ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi phung po yongs su rdzogs par byed pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / dam pa'i chos yongs su
58b1(mdo sde): bsrung ba sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi du byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu'o// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems
58b2(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa 'dri bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ phung po la mkhas pa sngon du 'gro ba dang khams la mkhas pa
58b3(mdo sde): sngon du 'gro ba dang / skye mched la mkhas pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / bden pa la mkhas pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / lta bar gyur pa
58b4(mdo sde): thams cad bsal ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / shes rab kyi dbang po sngon du 'gro ba dang / mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba/
58b5(mdo sde): sngon du 'gro ba dang / sgrib pa med pa'i ye shes mthong ba sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu'o//
58b6(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can gyi bsam pa dang /
58b7(mdo sde): bal 'jug pa sngon du 'grong dang / byams pa dang snying rje chen po sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can yongs su smin par bye ba la mi skyo ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la
59a1(mdo sde): 'jug pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / khyad par can gyi ye shes mthong ba khong du chud pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su byang bar bya ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / yongs/
59a2(mdo sde): su smin par bya ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / dngos po ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su rtogs pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems kyi stobs nye bar bsgrub pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i sa yongs su thob
59a3(mdo sde): par byed pa sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu'o// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems/
59a4(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste / sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa thibs po nye bar rgyu ba shes pa
59a5(mdo sde): sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i thibs po nye bar rgyu ba shes pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi dbang po thibs po nye bar rgyu ba shes pa sngon du 'gro dang /
59a6(mdo sde): sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / mos pa'i thibs po nye bar rgyu ba shes pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa dang / mos pa'i thibs
59a7(mdo sde): bonye bar shes pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams gsum gyi thabs ponye bar tu bshes pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang ngag lanyal gyi thibs po ci
59b1(mdo sde): bar rgyu ba shes pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi 'chi 'pho ba dang / skye ba thibs po nye bar rgyu ba shes pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi phung po gsum du rnam
59b2(mdo sde): par banag pa thibs po nye bar rgyu ba shes pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / dbang po mi skyo ba'i sems can yongs su smin par bya ba shis pa sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams
59b3(mdo sde): kyi sngon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu'o// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu ste/
59b4(mdo sde): bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad gzod ma nas 'byung ba med pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams cad gzod ma nas mtshan nyid med pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams cad gzod ma
59b5(mdo sde): nas skye ba med pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams cad gzod ma nas yod pa ma yin pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams cad gzod ma nas chags pa med pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos
59b6(mdo sde): thams cad 'jug pa med pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams cad ldog pa med pa'i sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams cad dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams
59b7(mdo sde): cad kyi thog ma dang / bar ma dang / tha ma mnyam pa nyid sngon du 'gro ba dang / chos thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid la 'jug pa'i rtog pa dang // rnam par rtog pa med pa sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu
60a1(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu'o// rigs kyi de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi sa/
60a2(mdo sde): rol tu phyin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad rnam par dbye ba la shin tu rnam par brtags pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / dkar po'i chos shin tu yongs
60a3(mdo sde): sku rdzogs pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / byang chub kyi tshogs bsags pa dpag tu med pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi tshogs chen po yongs su gzung ba sngon du 'gro ba dang /
60a4(mdo sde): snying rje chen po yengs pa khong du chud par bya ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dbye ba'i rim pas shes pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / sems can gyi khams dang / nyon mongs pa'i spyod pa la/
60a5(mdo sde): 'jug pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul la 'jug cing rjes su 'gro ba dang shes pa yid la byed pa sngon du 'gro ba dang / stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa dang /
60a6(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa la lhag par dmigs shing kun shes par bya ba sngon du 'gro ba dang / rnam pa thams cad kyi mchog dang ldan pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la dbang bskum
60a7(mdo sde): ba'i sa thob pa sngon du 'gro ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di'i sngon du 'gro ba'i chos rnam pa bcu'o// de la pha rol tu phyin pa'i don gang zhe na/
60b1(mdo sde): spyod pa'i khyad par yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i don ni pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// ye shes zab cing rgya che ba yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i don ni pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// 'dus
60b2(mdo sde): byas dang 'dus ma byas la chags pa med pa'i don ni pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// 'khor ba'i nyes pa ji lta ba bzhin du rdzogs pa'i don ni pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// skye bo mi mkhas pa
60b3(mdo sde): rnams khong du chud par byed pa'i don ni pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// chos kyi mdzod zad mi shes pa yang dag par ston pa'i don ni pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// sgrib pa med pa'i rnam par zur
60b4(mdo sde): pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// sems can gyi khams rab tu shes par bya ba'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// sbyin pa mnyam pa nyid rjes su rtogs pa'i
60b5(mdo sde): don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// tshul khrims mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// bzod pa mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i don
60b6(mdo sde): ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// brtson 'grus mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// bsam gtan mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i
60b7(mdo sde): pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la shes par mkhas pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// chos thams cad rab tu shes par bya ba'i don ni/
61a1(mdo sde): pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// phyir mi ldog pa'i sa yang dag par
61a2(mdo sde): thob par byed pa'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su sbyang ba'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya
61a3(mdo sde): nga'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// byang chub kyi snying po la sangs rgyas kyi ye shes yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// bdud thams cad gdul
61a4(mdo sde): bar bya ba'i don ni/ pha rol phyin pa'i don no// 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa gnyis su med par bstan cing sgrol ba'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// yon tan thams cad
61a5(mdo sde): kyi pha rol tu 'gro ba'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// bas kyi rgol ba thams cad tshar gcod pa'i don no/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa dang /
61a6(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i don ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i don ro// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i dor ni/
61a7(mdo sde): tubyin pa'i don no// blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu ngon par rdzogs par byang chub par byed pa'i don no// pha rol tu phyin pa'i don no// chos kyi 'khor lo rnam pa bcu
61b1(mdo sde): gnyis su bskor ba'i dor ni/ pha rol du phyin pa'i don no// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang po'i sna ltas nI/ spong bsum gyi
61b2(mdo sde): stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams gter bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gsum yongs su gang bar mthong ngo // rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i
61b3(mdo sde): sa gnyis pa'i snga lngas ni/ gang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams lag mthil lta bur gyur pa la/ rin po che bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du mas legs par brgyan par mthong ngo //
61b4(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i sa gsum pa'i snga ltas ni/ bdag nyid dpa' zhing lag cha dang / go cha sra ba thogs nas pas kyi rgol ba
61b5(mdo sde): thams cad 'dul bar mthong ngo // rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i sa banI pa'i snga lngas ni/ phyogs bzhi nas rlung gi dkyil 'a
61b6(mdo sde): bzhis thams cad dang ldan pa'i sa'i dkyil 'khor chen po la me tog sna tshogs kyis mngon du 'thor bar mthong ngo // rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang
61b7(mdo sde): chub sems dpa'i sa lnga pa'i snga ltas ni/ rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i bud med kyi mgo la me tog tsam pa ka'i 'phreng ba 'dogs par mthong ngo // rigs kyi de la byang
62a1(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i sa drug pa'i snga ltas ni rdzing themaskas pa ni dang ldan pa// gser gyi bye ma bdal bru rnyog
62a2(mdo sde): pa med cing dang la/ yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i chus yongs su gang po me tog ut+pal dang / ku mu da dang / pad+ma dkar pos brgyan pa'i chu mthong ste de la bdag nyid rtsi dgra' zhing yongs su
62a3(mdo sde): spyod par mthong ngo // rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i sa bdun pa'i snga ltas ni/ phyogs g.yas g.yon gnyis ni sems can dmyal
62a4(mdo sde): pa'i g.yang sa mthong ste/ de nas bdag nyid ma smas ma nyams par slar ldog pa mthong ngo // rigs kyi de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i sa brgyad pa'i
62a5(mdo sde): snga ltas ni/ phrag pa gnyis na ri dgas kyi rgyal po seng ge ral pa can cod pan thogs pa/ gcan gzin phra mo thams cad skrag par byed cing 'dug par mthong ngo // rigs kyi bu de la
62a6(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i sa dgu pa'i snga ltas ni/ 'khor lhos sbyar ba'i rgyal po mthong ste/ hU~M bo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag du mas yongs
62a7(mdo sde): sra bskor cing mdun gyis bltas la/ mgo'o spang na rin po che sna tshogs kyis spras pa'i gdugs dkar po 'dzin pa mthong ngo // rigs kyi bu ri la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
62b1(mdo sde): chen po'i byang chub sems dpa'i sna bcu pa'i snga las ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i su mthong ste/ kha dog gser lta bu'i 'od bdom gang ba/ tshangs pa bye ba d+mag khrig pa tu spyong brag drum
62b2(mdo sde): yongs su bskor zhing / mdun gyis bltas nas chos ston par mthong ste/ rigs kyi bu bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chubs sa bcu pod
62b3(mdo sde): snga ltas yin no// de la rigs kyi bu de ci'i phyir sa dang po la rab tu dga' ba zhes bya zhe na/ de ni thog mar 'jig rten las 'das pa'i sems sngon ma thob pa de mngon du gyur te/ don chen po'i bsam
62b4(mdo sde): pa phun sum tshogs pa'i phyir/ rab tu dga' ba chen po skye bas sa dang po la rab tu dga' ba zhes bya'o// lhung ba phra mo'i dri ma dang / tshul khrims kyi nyes pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'i phyir/
62b5(mdo sde): sa gnyis pa ni dri ma med pa zhes bya'o// tshad med pa'i ye shes dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi 'od snang ba de bskyod par mi nus shing / gang gis kyang zil gyis mi gnon pa dang / thos pa 'dzin pa'i
62b6(mdo sde): gzungs la gnas pa'i phyir sa gsum pa ni 'od byed pa zhes bya'o// shes rab kyi mes nyon mongs pa thams cad bsregs shing // byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos bsgoms pa'i me'i 'od 'phro ba cher gyur
62b7(mdo sde): pas/ sa bzhi pa ni 'od 'phro ba zhes bya'o// de bsgom pa'i thabs dang / mchog gi ye shes la dbang sgyur bar dka' ba dang / mthong ba dang / bsgoms pas spangs pa'i nyon mongs pa thub par dka' ba
63a1(mdo sde): rdul ba'i phyir/ sa lnga pa la shin tu sbyang dka' ba zhes bya'o// 'du byed kyi chos par chad med pa mngon du gyur te/ mtshan ma med pa yid la byed pa thams cad mngon/
63a2(mdo sde): du byed pa'i/ sa drug pa la mngon sum pa zhes bya'o// zag pa med pa'i chos rnams la bar chad med cing / mtshan ma med pa yid la byed pas// rnam par grol ba'i ting nge 'dzin la rgyun ring

83a1(mdo sde): yang byang chub sems dpa' rin chen 'od 'phro la/ tshangs pa chen pos 'di skad ces smras so// sems can ji snyed gcig gis chos zab mo 'di lta bu rtog/

83a3(mdo sde): pos smras pa// sprul pa de dag nyid kyang rang bzhin yod pa ma yin na/ de dag gi sems dang / sems las byung ba gang nas skyes par 'gyur/ smras pa gang chos kyi dbyings yod pa yang ma
83a4(mdo sde): yin/ med pa yang ma yin par yang dag par shes pa de dag gis/ zab mo de'i don shes par nus so// de nas tshangs pa chen pos/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to//
83a5(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' rin chen 'od ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ chos kyi gzhung zab mo 'di la mkhas pa lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa
83a6(mdo sde): de bzhin te/ tshangs pa chen po de ji ltar khyod kyis smras pa de bzhin no// byang chub sems dpa' rin chen 'od 'phro 'dis khyod la ji skad snyan pa bzhin du nan tan du sgrubs shig dang / mi
83a7(mdo sde): skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob par 'gyur ro// de nas lha'i rgyal po tshangs pa chen po dang / gzhan yang tshangs pa'i 'khor de dag stan las langs te ga bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar
83b1(mdo sde): nas dpus mo g.yas pa'i lda nga sa la btsugs te/ thal mo sbyar bas byang chub sems dpa' rin chen 'od 'phro'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ tshig 'di skad ces spras
83b2(mdo sde): so// deng skyes bu chen po khyod dang phrad cing bdag cag gis dam pa'i chos 'di lta bu thos par gyur pa ngo mtshar che lags so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ tshangs pa chen po la bka'
83b3(mdo sde): stsal pa/ byang chub sems dpa' rin chen 'od 'phro 'di ma 'ongs pa'i dus na/ rin po che'i 'od dpal gyi snying po zhes bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
83b4(mdo sde): pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ bla na med pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sbyar ba/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa sangs rgyas
83b5(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das su 'gyur ro zhes bka' stsal to// de skad ces bka' stsal pa de'i tshe/ byang chub sems dpa' khri phrag sum stong gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i/
83b6(mdo sde): byang chub las phyir mi ldog par gyur to// lha'i bu khri phrag brgyad stong dang / rgyal po dang / blon po la sogs pa tshad med grangs med pa rnams kyis/ rdul med cing rdul dang bral ba'i
83b7(mdo sde): chos la chos kyi mig rnam par dag par gyur to// de nas 'khor 'dus pa de'i nang na dge slong khri phrag lnga bcu byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa// byang chub kyi sems las phyir mi ldog par
84a1(mdo sde): sems pa de dag kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rin chen 'od 'phros chos bstan pa 'di thos nas/ byang chub kyi sems phyir zhing brtan pa dang / bsam gyis mi khyab pa/
84a2(mdo sde): bla na med pa'i smon lam yongs su rdzogs nas yang byang chub tu sems bskyed de/ so so nas rang rang gi gos gyon pa phud de/ byang chub sems dpa' la gsol nas/ bla na med pa'i mchog dam pa'i sems
84a3(mdo sde): bskyed de/ smon lam 'di skad ces gsol to// bdag cag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba ci mchis pa de dag thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo'o zhes smon lam btab bo//
84a4(mdo sde): tshangs pa chen po dge slong de dag gis/ bsod nams de la brten nas ji skad smras pa bzhin nan tan du bsgrubs nas/ bskal pa chen po dgu bcu 'das pa na/ 'khor ba las yongs su 'das pa'i
84a5(mdo sde): shes pa skyes par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ dge slong de dag la bka' stsal pa/ dge slong dag khyed bskal pa grangs med pa sum cu 'das pa'i 'og tu/ bla na med pa'i sangs
84a6(mdo sde): rgyas su 'gyur te/ bskal pa'i ming ni rgyal bar dga' ba'i 'od kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba/ yul gyi ming ni dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya bar dus gcig tu kun kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
84a7(mdo sde): tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ste/ de dag kun kyang mtshan smon lam rnam par bkod pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba yon tan gyi mtshan bcu yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan to// gzhan
84b1(mdo sde): yang tshangs pa chen po gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po gang nyan pa dang 'dzin pa de dag ni mthu dang / gzi brjid chen po dang ldan par 'gyur te/ dper na gang la la zhig gis/ thabs/
84b2(mdo sde): dang mi ldan pas pha rol tu phyin pa drug bsngal pa chen po brgyad stong du spyod pa bas/ gang rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig gis gser 'od dam pa'i mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po
84b3(mdo sde): 'di glegs bam du bris te zla ba phyed phyed cing sems rtse gcig tu byas te/ klog cing 'don na/ bsod nams kyi phung po 'di la bsod nams kyi phung po snga ma des brgya'i char yang nye bar mi bod pa
84b4(mdo sde): nas grangs su ba dang dper bskrun par yang mi bzod do// tshangs pa chen po de lta bas na/ khyod kyis rtag tu yid la bya zhing / nan tan du bsgrub pa dang / gzung zhing gzhan la yang dag par rgya
84b5(mdo sde): cher bstan par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sngon 'das pa'i dus na nga byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe/ ji ltar skyes bu dpa' bo g.yul ngor lus srog la mi blta/
84b6(mdo sde): ba bzhin du/ ngas kyang mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di gzung zhing 'dzin pa dang / klog cing 'don pa dang / gzhan la yang rgya cher yang dag par ston pa la thogs pa med par gyur to// tshangs
84b7(mdo sde): pa chen po dper na/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po 'jig rten na gnas kyi bar rin po che sna bdun yang med par yang mi 'gyur ro// gal te rgyal po mi bzhugs na/ rin po che sna bdun yang mod la
85a1(mdo sde): med par 'gyur ro// tshangs pa chen po de ltar de bzhin du/ gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di 'jig rten na gnas kyi bar dug/ blan med pa'i chos rin po che/
85a2(mdo sde): thams cad kyang nub par mi 'gyur ro// mdo sde'i dbang po 'di nam med pa na/ gzhan dag kyang nub par 'gyur ro// de lta bas na mdo sde'i rgyal po 'di sems rtse gcig tu byas te/ mnyan pa
85a3(mdo sde): dang / gzung ba dang / klog pa dang / gzhan dag la yang rgya cher bshad pa dang / yi ger 'drir 'jug pa dang / lus dang srog la mi blta bas ngal ba dang / dub pa khyad du gsod cing brtson 'grus
85a4(mdo sde): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa spyad par bya ste/ bsod nams kyi nang na mchog yin par nga'i 'khor rnams kyis kyang de bzhin du bslab cing nan tan du bya'o// de nas tshangs pa'i rgyal po chen po la sogs te//
85a5(mdo sde): tshangs pa'i 'khor grangs med pa dang / brgya byin lha'i dbang po dang / rgyal po chen po bzhi dang / gzhan yang gnod sbyin gyi dbang po la sogs pa de dag thams cad stan las langs te/ bla gos
85a6(mdo sde): phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis
85a7(mdo sde): kyang / gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di bsrung ba dang / yongs su rgyas par bgyi'o// chos 'di ston pa'i tshe bgegs dang / bar chad kun bsal te/ dge bar 'gyur ba dang
85b1(mdo sde): kha dog dang mthu yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba dang / spobs pa thogs pa med pa dang / lus dang sems bde bar 'gyur ba dang / de'i 'khor rnams kyang bde ba nyams su myong ba dang /
85b2(mdo sde): gang na gnas pa'i yul 'khor de yang mu ge dang dgra'i 'jigs pa dang / mi ma yin pas 'tshe ba zhig mchis na yang / bdag cag lha'i 'khor gyis yongs su bsrungs pas/ de dag bde zhing skyid/
85b3(mdo sde): pa dang / gnod pa rnams mi 'byung bar gyur na de dag kyang / bdag cag lha'i mthu lags par 'tshal bar bgyi'o// gang la la zhig mdo sde'i 'di la mchod cing rim gro bgyid na/ de la bdag cag
85b4(mdo sde): gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dang 'dra bar mchod cing rim gro bgyi'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis lha'i rgyal po tshangs pa chen po la sogs te/ tshangs pa'i 'khor de dag dang / rgyal
85b5(mdo sde): po chen po bzhi dang / gnod sbyin gyi dbang po la sogs pa rnams la legs so zhes bka' stsal te/ legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu khyod kyis dam pa'i chos zab mo 'di yang thos/ mdo/
85b6(mdo sde): sde'i dbang po 'di dang / 'di 'dzin pa la bsrung ba dang / bskyab pa'i sems bskyed pa des bsod nams kyi khyad par tshad med pa dang ldan pas/ myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs
85b7(mdo sde): pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ tshangs pa'i rgyal po la sogs pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la
86a1(mdo sde): mngon par bstod do// gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po las/ stong pa nyid la brten nas bsam pa yongs su rdzogs pa zhes bya ba'i/
86a2(mdo sde): le'u ste bcu pa'o// / de nas rgyal po chen po rnam thos kyi bu dang / rgyal po chen po yul 'khor srung dang / rgyal po chen po 'phags skyes po dang ga rgyal po chen po mig mi bzang
86a3(mdo sde): stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu bgos nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas kabacom ldan 'das la 'di skad
86a4(mdo sde): ces gsol to// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsungs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gzigs
86a5(mdo sde): pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis dgongs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs thams cad kyis yongs su bzung ba/ lha'i tshogs thams cad kyis phyag bgyis pa/ lha'i tshogs thams
86a6(mdo sde): cad kyis mchod pa dang / lha'i dbang po'i tshogs thams cad kyis mngon par bstod pa/ 'jig rten skyong ba thams cad kyis mchod cing bsngags te/ brjod nas rab tu bkur ba/ lha'i khang khyim
86a7(mdo sde): thams cad snang bar bgyis pa/ sems can thams cad la mchog tu bde ba thams cad rab tu sbyin par bgyid pa/ sems can dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro'i skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig
86b1(mdo sde): rten gyi sdug bsngal thams cad skems pa/ 'jigs pa thams cad kyi rgyun gcod pa/ pha rol gyi dmag tshogs thams cad rab tu zlog pa/ mu ge'i yang ba thams cad rab tu zhi bar bgyid pa
86b2(mdo sde): nad kyi yang ba thams cad rab tu zhi bar bgyid pa/ gza'i gnod pa thams cad sel ba/ mchog tu zhi bar bgyid pa/ mya ngan dang nyon mongs pa thams cad rab tu zhi bar bgyid pa ka gnod
86b3(mdo sde): pa rnam pa sna tshogs rab tu zhi bar bgyid pa/ gnod pa 'bum rab tu zhi bar bgyid pa la sogs so// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di 'khor gyi
86b4(mdo sde): nang du rgya cher yang dag par rab tu bshad na chos mnyan pa chos bdud rtsi'i khu ba 'dis bdag cag rgyal po chen po dpung dang g.yog tu bcas pa bzhi'i lha'i lus 'di gzi byin chen pos rnam par 'phel
86b5(mdo sde): bar 'gyur ro// bdag cag gi lus la brtson pa dang / stobs dang mthu yang skyed par 'gyur/ gzi brjid dang / dpal dang / phun sum tshogs pa yang bdag cag gi lus la 'jug par
86b6(mdo sde): 'gyur te/ btsun pa bcom ldan 'das bdag cag rgyal po chen po bzhi ni chos dang ldan pa/ chos smra ba/ chos kyi rgyal po lags te/ btsun pa bcom ldan 'das bdag cag ni chos kyis lha dang /
86b7(mdo sde): klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / dri za dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po rnams kyi rgyal po bgyi'o// 'byung po'i tshogs mi bzad pa/ snying rje ma mchis pa/
87a1(mdo sde): gzhan gyi gzi byin 'phrog pa rnams bzlog par bgyi'o// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das bdag cag rgyal po chen po bzhis gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po nyi shu rtsa brgyad dang /
87a2(mdo sde): gnod sbyin 'bum phrag du ma dang lhan cig tu rtag par rgyun du lha'i mig rnam par dag pa mi las 'das pas/ 'dzam bu'i gling thams cad la blta bar bgyi/ bsrung bar bgyi/ yongs su bskyang bar
87a3(mdo sde): bgyi ste btsun pa bcom ldan 'das de'i slad du/ bdag cag rgyal po chen po bzhi 'jig rten skyong ba zhes ming du chags so// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das gang su dag 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir pha rol
87a4(mdo sde): gyi dmag tshogs kyis yul 'joms par 'gyur ram/ mu ge'i yang ba 'am/ nad kyi yang ba 'am/ gnod pa sna tshogs brgya dang / gnod pa spong dang / gnod pa 'bum dag gis
87a5(mdo sde): gtses par gyur pa na/ btsun pa bcom ldan 'das bdag cag rgyal po chen po bzhis gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di 'dzin pa'i dge slong chos smra ba de dag la bskul
87a6(mdo sde): bar bgyi'o// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das nam bdag cag rgyal po chen po bzhis rdzu 'phrul dang / byin gyis brlabs kyis dge slong chos smra ba de dag bskul ba na/ yul gang dang gang du mchi bar//
87a7(mdo sde): gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di yul de dang de dag tu rgya cher yang dag par ston par 'gyur te/ gang gnod pa sna rogs brgya dang / gnod pa sna tshogs stong yul du 'byung ba 'di lta bu 'di dag
87b1(mdo sde): rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ro// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das mi'i rgyal po gang gis yul du mdo sde'i dbang po 'dzin pa'i dge slong chos smra ba de dag mchi bar 'gyur ba'i yul de dag tu gser 'od dam pa mdo
87b2(mdo sde): sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di yang bsnyen par 'gyur ro// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das nam mi'i rgyal pos gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di mnyan te/ de thos nas mdo sde'i dbang po
87b3(mdo sde): 'dzin pa'i dge slong de dag phyir rgol ba thams cad las kun tu srung bar bgyid/ yongs su sgrub pa dang / yongs su 'dzin pa dang / yongs su skyong bar bgyid na/ btsun pa bcom ldan 'das
87b4(mdo sde): bdag cag rgyal po chen po bzhis/ mi'i rgyal po de'i yul thams cad na gnas pa'i sems can rnams kun tu bsrung bar bgyi/ yongs su bskyab pa dang / yongs su gzung ba dang / yongs su
87b5(mdo sde): bskyang ba dang / zhi ba dang bde legs su 'gyur bar bgyi'o// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das mi'i rgyal pos nam dge slong ngam/ dge slong ma 'am/ dge bsnyen nam/ dge bsnyen ma mdo sde'i dbang po
87b6(mdo sde): 'dzin pa la/ bde bar sbyar ba thams cad kyis bde bar bgyid na/ btsun pa bcom ldan 'das bdag cag rgyal po chen po bzhis mi'i rgyal po de'i yul thams cad na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la
87b7(mdo sde): bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis bde ba dang yo byad thams cad phun sum tshogs par bgyi'o// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das nam mi'i rgyal pos dge slong ngam// dge slong ma 'am/ dge bsnyen nam
88a1(mdo sde): dge bsnyen ma mdo sde'i dbang po 'di 'dzin pa la/ bsti sbrang du bgyid/ bla mar bgyid/ rim gror bgyid cing mchod na/ btsun pa bcom ldan 'das bdag cag rgyal po chen/
88a2(mdo sde): po bzhis mi'i rgyal po chen po de la/ rgyal po thams cad pas ches bsti stang du bgyi/ ches bla mar bgyi/ ches mchod par bgyi sde/ yul thams cad du yang rab tu bsngags par bgyi'o//

88a4(mdo sde): kyis rgyal po chen po bzhi la legs so zhes bya ba byin te/ rgyal po chen po dag legs so legs so// rgyal po chen po khyed yang legs so legs so// 'di lta ste/ khyed ni sngon gyi rgyal ba la lhag par
88a5(mdo sde): bya ba byas pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams bskyed pa/ sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa/ chos dang ldan pa/ chos smra ba/ chos kyi rgyal po/ chos kyis lha dang mi rnams
88a6(mdo sde): kyi rgyal po byed pa'o// 'di lta ste/ khyed ni yun ring por sems can thams cad la phan pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ bde ba dang / byams pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la phan pa dang /
88a7(mdo sde): bde bar bya ba'i lhag pa'i bsam pa la zhugs pa/ mi phan pa thams cad 'gog pa/ sems can thams cad la bde ba thams cad nye bar bsgrub par brtson pa yin te/ rgyal po chen po khyed
88b1(mdo sde): bzhis mi'i rgyal po gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di la mchod pa dang / rim gror byed par brjon pa de dag la kun tu bsrung bar gyis shig/ yongs su bskyad pa dang
88b2(mdo sde): yongs su gzung ba dang yongs su bskyang ba dang / zhi ba dang bde legs su 'gyur ba gyis shig/ des na rgyal po chen po dpung dang g.yog dang / gnod sbyin 'bum phrag du ma dang bcas pa khyed bzhis
88b3(mdo sde): 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi tshul kun tu srung bar 'gyur ro// yongs su sbyang ba dang / yongs su gzung bar yang 'gyur ro//

89a1(mdo sde): gcig tu bgos nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lhangs la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das gal bde logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di ska/

89a4(mdo sde): lnga'i dbang po'i dam tshig rgyal po'i bstan bcos 'dis rgyal po bgyid cing rtag par rgyun du gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po 'di nyan tam/ rim gro bgyid dam/ mchod pa bgyid dam/

89b1(mdo sde): bgyid par 'gyur/ bdag cag gi gzi byin dang / dpal dang / phun sum tshogs pa yang rnam par 'phel bar 'gyur ro// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das bdag cag rgyal poran/

102a6(mdo sde): par ma mchis shing mi rdzi bar 'gyur ba dang / ci nas mi'i rgyal po de dag gis/ rang rang gi yul rnams su chos kyi sgron ma chen po 'bar bar bgyis shing / snang bar bgyis par 'gyur ba dang /
